1. The flushing capacity of the toilet is not very good. It takes three or four flushes for the large toilet to flush it clean, and two flushes for the small toilet. The flush button must be pressed all the time, otherwise the water will stop flushing. The toilet problem was the most uncomfortable thing about this stay. I don‚Äôt want to call the hotel to complain on the spot. I guess I have the same hardware problem when changing rooms, which is very annoying.
2. The air conditioning is not powerful and it is hot and stuffy.
3. There is a sanitary blind spot in the shower bathroom, as shown in the picture.
4. The towels are hard and not white, not like the quality of a five-star hotel.
5. Two people in a twin room are only given a set of small bottles of shampoo and body soap. Fortunately, I have a spare set. I don‚Äôt want to call the hotel to ask for an extra set, which is annoying.
6. The check-in order included a welcome fruit, but when I checked in at nearly three o'clock in the afternoon, I found that there was no welcome fruit. Because I drove from Jiuzhaigou to Chengdu early in the morning and didn't eat lunch, I originally wanted to eat some welcome fruit to satisfy my hunger, but it turned out that there was no welcome fruit. I mustered up the courage to get it. I called to ask for it, and they got back to me in half an hour. But after waiting and waiting, I didn‚Äôt come, so I went out to the museum. When I came back in the evening, I saw a small plate of fruit on the table, two small pears and a small orange, three Together they are not as big as my palm. I thought that hotels are having a hard time now, and they are so picky about delivering fruits. However, the hotel in Xishuangbanna is better. They give fruits as generously as if they are free.
7. I wore short-sleeved shorts and pajamas to sleep. When I woke up in the morning, I found two holes in my hands and legs, which looked like bites from some insect. I opened the quilt and searched for a long time but found nothing. It was so strange.
8. The cleaning lady is very enthusiastic and greets me warmly when I meet her.

In short, the price/performance ratio of a hotel worth 1,000 yuan per night is not as good as that of 700 yuan, which is disappointing.
